                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial"><span>Question 93</span></div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>Select the word or phrase that is most closely opposite in meaning to the capitalized word: AVARICE</p>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Generosity</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Conservation</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Indulgence</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">

</label>
                                                
                                            </div>

                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Avarice- লিপ্সা। Option গুলোর মধ্যে Generosity- মহত্ব। Conservation- রক্ষণশীলতা। Indulgence- প্রশ্রয় দেয়া, Cupidity- লিপ্সা। অর্থের দিক থেকে Avarice ও Generosity- শব্দদ্বয় বিপরীতার্থক।</p>
</span>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Abstract noun love -এর পূর্বে কোনো article বসে না আর such + a/an + noun বসে। Beautiful যেহেতু consonant দিয়ে শুরু সুতরাং such a beautiful thing হবে।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>No article, no article</p>

                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>The, no article</p>

                                            </div>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>ধর্মগ্রন্থের পূর্বে article the বসে এবং adjective-এর superlative degree -এর পূর্বে the বসে।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Extract (বলপ্রয়োগের মাধ্যমে বের করে আনা) -এর বিপরীত শব্দ Insert যার অর্থ নিবিষ্ট, ঢোকানো। তাছাড়া Quest অর্থ খোঁজা, তল্লাশি করা, Select অর্থ নির্বাচন করা আর Collect অর্থ সংগ্রহ করা।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>

                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p><u>How the man died </u>&nbsp;is a mystery. The underlined clause is an example&nbsp; of-</p>

                                        </div>

                                            </div>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Noun clause</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Adjective clause</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Adverbial clause</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Co-ordinate clause</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Noun clause কারণ এখানে মারা যাওয়ার ঘটনা জিজ্ঞেস করা হচ্ছে অর্থাৎ একটি noun দিয়ে বলা হচ্ছে, তাই এটি noun clause। What দিয়ে question করলে answer এ noun পাওয়া যায়।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Be surprised at something&nbsp;অর্থ কোনো বিষয়ে আশ্চর্য হওয়া। সুতরাং শূন্যস্থানে at বসবে।</p>

                                    </div>
                            </div>

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>দুটি clause পরস্পর বিপরীত ধারণা প্রদানের জন্য although conjunction টি ব্যবহৃত হয়। Although যোগে বাক্যটির বাংলা: যদিও ছুটির দিন ছিল তবুও ডাক্তার হৃদরোগীর উপর জরুরি শল্য চিকিৎসা চালালেন।</p>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Is your payment found too little to you?</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">

                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Are your payment found too little by you?</p>

                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Passive voice এ obj এবং&nbsp;sub. interchange হয়। তাই object your payment হয়ে গেলো subject. যেহেতু present tense এবং&nbsp;singular number তাই do এর পরিবর্তে use হবে is। যেটি interrogative question হওয়ার কারণে বাক্যের শুরুতে&nbsp;use হবে।</p>

                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>By whom the door was opened?</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Past Indefinite tense 'who' যুক্ত interrogative বাক্যের passive form -এর structure By whom + was/were + obj কে sub + verb এর p.p + interrogative mark।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="row questionBlock">

                            <div class="row question">
                                <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial"><span>Question 138</span></div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>The passive form of the sentence- 'We can gain nothing without labour'.</p>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Nothing is not be gained without labour.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Nothing is to be gained without labour by us.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Nothing can not be gained without labour.&nbsp;</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Nothing can be gained without labour.</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Modal auxiliary verb যুক্ত বাক্যকে passive voice -এ রূপান্তরের structure: obj কে sub + modal auxiliary verb + be + verb&nbsp;-এর p.p+ by + obj কে sub + বাকি অংশ। সুতরাং বাক্যটির সঠিক passive voice : Nothing can be gained (by us না থাকলেও চলে) without labour।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="row questionBlock">

                            <div class="row question">
                                <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial"><span>Question 139</span></div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>In an admission test, to answer correctly/accurately is more important than_____.&nbsp;</p>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>you finish quickly</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>finishing quickly</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>quick finish</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>to finish quickly</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>'to finish quickly' is the correct expression for the sentence. 'to finish quickly' যোগে বাক্যটির বাংলা- ভর্তি পরীক্ষায় দ্রুত শেষ করার চেয়ে সঠিক উত্তর দেয়া বেশি গুরুত্বপূর্ণ।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                            <div class="row question">
                                <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial"><span>Question 140</span></div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>He said, "Good morning, can you help me?" (Indirect)</p>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>He wished him good morning and asked whether he could help him.</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>He wished him good morning and asked for help.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>He told good morning and asked whether he can help him.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>He wished him good morning and asked to help him.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Reported speech এ good morning এবং interrogative বাক্য থাকলে structure হবে sub + wished + someone + good morning + and + asked + whether/if + sub + can -এর past form could + প্রশ্নবোধক বাক্যের sub -এর বাকি অংশ।&nbsp;</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>

                            <div class="row question">
                                <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial"><span>Question 142</span></div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>He saw the girl and fell in love immediately. (make it complex)</p>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>As soon as he saw the girl, he fell in love with her.</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Seeing the girl, he fell in love quickly.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Seeing the girl, immediately he fell in love.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>He fell in love soon after seeing the girl.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Complex বাক্যে দুটি clause থাকে যাদের মধ্যে একটি principal clause এবং আরেকটি subordinate clause। সুতরাং প্রদত্ত বাক্যটির complex রূপ হলো As soon as he saw the girl, he fell in love with her।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Obdurate</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Docile</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Impertinent</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Intractable</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>

                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>'Stubborn' (একগুঁয়ে, জেদি) -এর একই অর্থবোধক শব্দ হলো- Obdurate। তাছাড়া Docile অর্থ সহজে বশ মানে এমন, বাধ্য, Impertinent অর্থ অপ্রাসঙ্গিক, অসঙ্গত আর Intractable অর্থ সহজে নিয়ন্ত্রণ করা যায় না এমন, দুর্দান্ত।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>Find out this <u>text</u> in your <u>text</u> book. The underlined words are respectively:&nbsp;</p>

                                        </div>

                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">

                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>noun and noun</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">

                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>noun and adverb</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>adjective and noun</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>noun and adjective</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>প্রথম text অর্থ কোনো নির্দিষ্ট লিখা/অংশ; so এটি noun। আর দ্বিতীয় 'text' অর্থ কোনো নির্দিষ্ট পাঠ্য বই।&nbsp;text book ছাড়াও reference book বা বিভিন্ন বই থাকে, তাই এটি adjective।</p>
